Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsProductivityAmazing Marvin\nAmazing Marvin\n\nThe Amazing Marvin modules allow you to create, update, search, retrieve, and delete tasks from your Amazing Marvin account.\n\nGetting Started with Amazing Marvin\n\nPrerequisites\n\nAn Amazing Marvin account - create an account at amazingmarvin.com/.\n\nConnecting Amazing Marvin to Make\n\nTo connect your Amazing Marvin account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Amazing Marvin account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\nGo to URL Address, Amazing Marvin API Credentials\n\nCopy the API Key to your clipboard\n\nLog in to your Make account, and add a module from the Amazing Marvin app into Make scenario.\n\nClick Add next to the Connection field.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field,  enter the details copied in step 3 and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nConnecting Amazing Marvin database to Make\n\nThe Update a Task, Search Tasks, Delete a Task, Get a Task, and Make an API Call modules require a database connection with Amazing Marvin. You need to obtain API credentials from Amazing Marvin.\n\nLog in to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\nGo to URL Address, Amazing Marvin API Credentials\n\nCopy the syncUser, syncPassword, syncServer, and syncDatabase fields. Keep this open in a separate tab or browser for easier copy-pasting.\n\nLog in to your Make account, and add a module from the Amazing Marvin app into Make scenario.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Username field, enter the syncUser key.\n\nIn the Password field, enter the syncPassword key.\n\nIn the Database URL field, enter the syncServer key.\n\nIn the Database Name field, enter the syncDatabase key.\n\nTask\n\nYou can create, update, search, delete, and retrieve tasks using the following modules.\n\nCreate a Task\n\nCreates a new task.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\n\n\n\nDone\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the task needs to be done.\n\n\n\n\nDay\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the day on which the task is to be executed.\n\n\n\n\nTitle\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a title for the task to create.\n\n\n\n\nParent ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a Parent ID for the task to create.\n\n\n\n\nLabel IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Label IDs to add to the task.\n\n\n\n\nFirst Scheduled\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the scheduled date for the task.\n\n\n\n\nRank\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the rank for the task to update.\n\n\n\n\nDaily Section\n\n\t\n\nSelect the daily section for the task:\n\nMorning \n\nAfternoon\n\nEvening\n\n\n\n\nBonus Section\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the bonus sections for the task.\n\n\n\n\nNote\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the note for the task being created.\n\n\n\n\nDue Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the due date to create the task.\n\nUpdate a Task\n\nUpdates a task.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\n\n\n\nUsername\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the syncUser details of your account.\n\n\n\n\nPassword\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the syncPassword details of your account.\n\n\n\n\nDatabase URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the syncServer details of your account.\n\n\n\n\nDatabase Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the syncDatabase details of your account.\n\n\n\n\nTask ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Task ID to update a task.\n\n\n\n\nDone\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the task needs to be done.\n\n\n\n\nDay\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the day on which the task is to be executed.\n\n\n\n\nTitle\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a title for the task to create.\n\n\n\n\nParent ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a Parent ID for the task to update.\n\n\n\n\nLabel IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Label IDs to add to the task.\n\n\n\n\nFirst Scheduled\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the updated scheduled date for the task.\n\n\n\n\nRank\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the rank for the task to update.\n\n\n\n\nDaily Section\n\n\t\n\nSelect the daily section for the task:\n\nMorning \n\nAfternoon\n\nEvening\n\n\n\n\nBonus Section\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the bonus sections for the task.\n\n\n\n\nNote\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the updated note for the task.\n\n\n\n\nDue Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the due date to create the task.\n\nSearch Tasks\n\nSearches for a specific task or lists them all.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\n\n\n\nDone\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the task needs to be done.\n\n\n\n\nDay\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the day on which the task was executed to search.\n\n\n\n\nTitle\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a title for the task to search.\n\n\n\n\nParent ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a Parent ID for the task to search.\n\n\n\n\nLabel IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Label IDs to search the task.\n\n\n\n\nFirst Scheduled\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the scheduled date of the task to retrieve.\n\n\n\n\nRank\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the rank of the task to search.\n\n\n\n\nDaily Section\n\n\t\n\nSelect the daily section for the task:\n\nMorning \n\nAfternoon\n\nEvening\n\n\n\n\nBonus Section\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the bonus sections for the task.\n\n\n\n\nNote\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the note for the task being created.\n\n\n\n\nDue Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the due date of the task to search.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of tasks Make should return during one execution cycle. The default value is 10.\n\nDelete a Task\n\nDeletes a task.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\n\n\n\nTask ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Task ID to delete a task.\n\nGet a Task\n\nReturns a certain task.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\n\n\n\nTask ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Task ID to retrieve a task.\n\nOthers\nMake an API Call\n\nMakes an API request to Database using CouchDB API\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Amazing Marvin account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://512940bf-6e0c-4d7b-884b-9fc66185836b-bluemix.cloudant.com\n\nFor example: /_all_docs\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the CouchDB API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET\n\nto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST\n\nto create a new entry.\n\nPUT\n\nto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH\n\nto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE\n\nto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List\n\nThe following API call returns all documents from your Amazing Marvin account:\n\nURL: /_all_docs\n\nMethod: GET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > rows. \n\nIn our example, 56 documents were returned:\n\nAmazing Marvin\nGetting Started with Amazing Marvin\nConnecting Amazing Marvin to Make\nConnecting Amazing Marvin database to Make\nTask\nCreate a Task\nUpdate a Task\nSearch Tasks\nDelete a Task\nGet a Task\nOthers\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Scheduling\n\nWith Acuity Scheduling modules in Make, you can manage the appointments, clients, certificates, orders, off time, and availability in your Acuity Scheduling account.\n\nTo use the Acuity Scheduling modules, you must have an Acuity Scheduling account. You can create an account at acuityscheduling.com.\n\nRefer to the Acuity Scheduling API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Acuity Scheduling to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add an Acuity Scheduling module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom app client credentials. For more information, refer to the Acuity Scheduling OAuth2 page.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/acuity-scheduling\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nNote: Squarespace has acquired Acuity Scheduling. You can use either login credentials to connect Make to Squarespace Scheduling or Acuity Scheduling.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Acuity Scheduling modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Acuity Scheduling Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nAppointment\n\nWatch Appointments\n\nList Appointment Types\n\nGet Appointment\n\nCreate Appointment\n\nList Appointments\n\nUpdate Appointment\n\nReschedule Appointment\n\nCancel Appointment\n\nList Appointment Addons\n\nClient\n\nList Clients\n\nCreate Client\n\nUpdate Client\n\nDelete Client\n\nCertificate\n\nAdd Certificate Code\n\nList Certificate Codes\n\nDelete Certificate Codes\n\nCheck Certificate\n\nOrder\n\nWatch Orders\n\nList Orders\n\nGet Order\n\nBlock Off Time\n\nAdd Block Off Time\n\nList Block Off Time\n\nGet Block Off Time\n\nDelete Block Off Time\n\nAvailability\n\nList Available Classes\n\nCheck Available Times\n\nList Available Dates\n\nList Available Times\n\nOther\n\nList Payments\n\nList Intake Forms\n\nList Labels\n\nList Package Products\n\nMake an API Call\n\nNote\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nWhen you create a Acuity Scheduling webhook in Make, it is attached automatically and requires no additional set up.\n\nAcuity Scheduling\nConnect Acuity Scheduling to Make\nBuild Acuity Scheduling Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

AgilePlace modules in Make, you can create, manage, and monitor all your cards, tasks, users, comments, and boards in your AgilePlace account.\n\nTo get started with AgilePlace, create an account at planview.com/products-solutions/products/agileplace.\n\nConnect AgilePlace to Make\n\nTo make a connection you must obtain an API key from your Leankit account.\n\nLog in to your AgilePlace account.\n\nClick your avatar in the top-right corner, then click API Tokens.\n\nCreate a new token and copy it to your clipboard.\n\nGo to your Make scenario and select the AgilePlace module you want Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingZoho Campaigns\nZoho Campaigns\n\nWith Zoho Campaigns modules in Make, you can:\n\nwatch, list, create, send, clone, and delete campaigns, and retrieve a campaign report\n\nwatch contacts, watch unsubscribes, subscribe a contact, add contacts to a list, move a contact to do-not-mail, and unsubscribe a contact\n\ncreate, update, and delete mailing list\n\nTo get started with Zoho Campaigns, create an account at zoho.com\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Zoho Campaigns API documentation.\n\nConnect Zoho Campaigns to Make\n\nTo connect Zoho Campaigns app, you need to obtain the user credentials from your Zoho Campaigns account and insert them in the Zoho Campaigns module scenario.\n\nLog in to your Zoho Campaigns account.\n\nLog in to your Make account, insert a Zoho Campaigns module scenario, and click the Add button next to the Connection field.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Region field, select your region and click Save.\n\nEnter your email address associated with the Zoho account and click Next.\n\nEnter your Zoho account password and click Sign-in.\n\nWhen prompted to manage your domains, click Manage Domains or Skip for now.\n\nClick Accept to allow Make access data in your Zoho account.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now begin editing your scenario and adding more Zoho Campaigns modules. If your connection needs reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Zoho Campaign Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform following actions:\n\nWatch Campaigns\n\nTriggers when a campaign is under review, reviewed, stopped, canceled, paused, resumed, sent, or A/B test is completed.\n\nList Campaigns\n\nRetrieves a list of campaigns.\n\nCreate a Campaign\n\nCreates a new campaign.\n\nSend a Campaign\n\nSends an existing campaign by its key.\n\nClone a Campaign\n\nClones an existing campaign by its key.\n\nDelete a Campaign\n\nDeletes an existing campaign by its key.\n\nGet a Campaign Report\n\nRetrieves the detail report of a campaign by its key.\n\nWatch Contacts\n\nTriggers when a new contact is added to the mailing list.\n\nWatch Unsubscribes\n\nTriggers when a contact unsubscribed from any mailing list.\n\nSubscribe a Contact\n\nSubscribes a new contact or updates an existing contact in a mailing list.\n\nAdd Contacts to a List\n\nAdds multiple existing contacts to a mailing list by their emails.\n\nMove a Contact to Do-Not-Mail\n\nMoves an existing contact to Do-Not-Mail list by its email.\n\nUnsubscribe a Contact\n\nUnsubscribes an existing contact from a list by its email.\n\nCreate a Mailing List\n\nCreaes a new mailing list with contacts.\n\nUpdate a Mailing List\n\nUpdates an existing mailing list by its key.\n\nDelete a Mailing List\n\nDeletes an existing mailing list by its ID.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nZoho Campaigns\nConnect Zoho Campaigns to Make\nBuild Zoho Campaign Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Loyalty\n\nWith Yotpo - Loyalty modules in Make, you can watch loyalty events, create or update a customer record, and retrieve a customer.\n\nTo get started with Yotpo - Loyalty, create an account at yotpo.com.\n\nConnect Yotpo - Loyalty to Make\n\nTo connect Yotpo - Loyalty app, you need to obtain the GUID and API Key from your Yotpo - Loyalty account and insert them into your Make scenario.\n\nLog in to your Yotpo - Loyalty account.\n\nClick Settings. Follow the steps below to set them up.\n\nOpen the Watch Loyalty Events module, create a connection, click Save, ad copy the URL address to your clipboard, click OK and save the trigger.\n\nLog in to your Yotpo - Loyallty account.\n\nClick Settings and navigate to the Webhook URL.\n\nEnter the Webhook URL copied in step 1 and click Save.\n\nYou have successfully added the webhooks.\n\nYotpo - Loyalty\nConnect Yotpo - Loyalty to Make\nCustomers\nWatch Loyalty Events\nCreate or Update a Customer Record\nGet a Customer\nOther\nMake an API Call\nSetting up Yotpo - Loyalty Webhooks\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create a Viral Loops account at viral-loops.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Viral Loops to Make\n\nTo connect your Viral Loops account to Make you need to obtain the API Token from your Viral Loops account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your Viral Loops account.\n\nOpen the campaign for which you want to establish a connection and click Edit > Installation.\n\nCopy the API Token to your clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the Viral Loops module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Token field, enter the API key details copied in step 3, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nMilestone Campaigns\nWatch New Participant\nWatch New Reward\nWatch Reached Milestone\nRegister a User\nList Participants Data\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Participants\nConnecting Viral Loops Webhook using Make\n\nOpen any Watch module, establish a connection as mentioned in the respective modules, Click OK, and copy the URL address to your clipboard. Save the trigger.\n\nLog in to your Viral Loops account. Go to the Campaign in which you want to add the webhook.\n\nClick Edit > Integration > Enable the Webhook.\n\nEnable the endpoint, in the Endpoint URL field, enter the URL address copied in step 1, and click Save.\n\nThe webhook is added successfully.\n\nViral Loops\nGetting Started with Viral Loops\nConnecting Viral Loops to Make\nMilestone Campaigns\nWatch New Participant\nWatch New Reward\nWatch Reached Milestone\nRegister a User\nList Participants Data\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Participants\nConnecting Viral Loops Webhook using Make\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingUseINBOX\nUseINBOX\n\nWith UseINBOX modules in Make, you can manage the segments, contacts, contact lists, campaigns, and tags in your UseINBOX account.\n\nTo use the UseINBOX modules, you must have a UseINBOX account. You can create an account at useinbox.com.\n\nRefer to the UseINBOX API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect UseINBOX to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a UseINBOX module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Username and Password fields, enter your UseINBOX account's user credentials.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more UseINBOX modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet Up UseINBOX Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd an UseINBOX instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nClick OK and then Run once.\n\nLog in to your UseINBOX account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Settings.\n\nClick Webhooks.\n\nClick Create Webhook.\n\nIn the Url field, Paste the webhook URL you copied in step 4.\n\nClick Check Availability to test URL first.\n\nIn the Trigger field, select Contact Added.\n\nOptional: Enter a description for the webhook.\n\nClick Save.\n\nUseINBOX will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild UseINBOX Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nTriggers\n\nWatch Segments\n\nWatch Unsubscribed Contacts\n\nWatch Updated Contacts\n\nWatch Tags\n\nWatch New Contacts\n\nActions\n\nAdd a Contact To a List\n\nCreate a Contact List\n\nSend a Campaign\n\nUpdate Contact\n\nMark Contact as Unsubscribed\n\nMake an API Call\n\nUseINBOX\nConnect UseINBOX to Make\nSet Up UseINBOX Webhooks\nBuild UseINBOX Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

However this may have changed, so please see the X Developer Apps documentation for the most up-to-date directions.\n\nEstablish the connection with X (formerly Twitter) in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add an X (formerly Twitter) module to your scenario, and click the Add button next to the Connection field.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Client ID and Client Secret fields, enter the client credentials retrieved from your custom app.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingTikTok\nTikTok\n\nTikTok allows you to watch, create, update, list, and retrieve the ads, and video posts in your TikTok account.\n\nGetting Started with TikTok\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA TikTok account - create an account at tiktok.com.\n\nConnecting TikTok to Make\n\n1. Log in to your Make account, add a module from the TikTok app into an Make scenario.\n\n2. Click Add next to the Connection field.\n\n3. Authenticate your TikTok account.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nTikTok Ad\n\nYou can watch search, retrieve ads, update ads status, and list ad reports,\n\nWatch Ads\n\nTriggers when an ad is created or updated.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nWatch Ads\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the option to watch the ads:\n\nBy Created Time\n\nBy Updated Time\n\n\n\n\nAdvertiser ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Advertiser ID you want to watch.\n\n\n\n\nFilter\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the options to filter the ads based on the specified matches.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Campaign ID whose ads you want to watch.\n\n\n\n\nAd Group IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Ad Group IDs whose ads you want to watch.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of ads Make should return during one execution cycle. The default value is 2.\n\nSearch Ads\n\nSearches for Ads.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nAdvertiser ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Advertiser ID whose details you want to search.\n\n\n\n\nFilter\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the options to filter the ads based on the specified match.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Campaign ID whose ads you want to search.\n\n\n\n\nAd Group IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Ad Group IDs whose ads you want to search.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of ads Make should return during one execution cycle. The default value is 10.\n\nList Ad Reports\n\nRetrieves a list of TikTok ad reports.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nAdvertiser ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Advertiser ID whose ad reports you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nService Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the service type to list the specific service ad reports.\n\n\n\n\nReport Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the report type whose ad reports you want to list. For example, Basic Report.\n\n\n\n\nData Level\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the data level for the reports you want to list. For example, Auction Ad.\n\n\n\n\nDimensions\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the dimensions to include in the report. For example, Campaign ID.\n\n\n\n\nMetrics\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the attribute metrics to generate the report. For example, campaign name.\n\n\n\n\nLifetime\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to list the lifetime ad reports.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of ad reports Make should return during one execution cycle. The default value is 10.\n\nGet an Ad\n\nGets a specified ad.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nAdvertiser ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Advertiser ID whose ad details you want to retrieve.\n\n\n\n\nAd ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Ad ID whose details you want to retrieve.\n\nUpdate an Ad's Status\n\nUpdates an existing ad's status.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nAdvertiser ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Advertiser ID whose ad status you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nAd ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Ad ID whose status you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nOpt Status\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the status of the ad:\n\nEnable\n\nDisable\n\nDelete\n\nTikTok\n\nYou can watch and list TikTok video posts, retrieve embedded videos, and upload sounds with the following modules.\n\nWatch TikTok Video Posts\n\nTriggers when you upload a new TikTok video post.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of video posts Make should return during one execution cycle. The default value is 5.\n\nList TikTok Video Posts\n\nRetrieves a list of your public TikTok video posts.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of video posts Make should return during one execution cycle. The default value is 10.\n\nGet an Embedded Video\n\nReturns the embed code and information about the video.\n\nVideo URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the video URL address you want to embed.\n\nUpload a Sound\n\nUploads an original sound into TikTok.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nSource File\n\n\t\n\nAdd the sound details to upload to the video:\n\nFile NameEnter (map) the audio file including the extension. For example, invoice.mp3. The supported file types are mp3, wav, flac.The size of the uploaded music file must be less than 50 MB and the duration of the music file must be greater than 10 seconds and less than 300 seconds.\n\nDataEnter (map) the data of the file.\n\nOther\n\nYou can call APIs with the following module.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your TikTok account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://business-api.tiktok.com/open_api For example: /v1.2/ad/get\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the TikTok Developer Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGETto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOSTto create a new entry.\n\nPUTto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCHto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETEto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Ads\n\nThe following API call returns all the ads from your TikTok account:\n\nURL:/v1.2/ad/get\n\nMethod:GET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > data > list. You can create an account at stamped.io.\n\nRefer to the Stamped.io API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Stamped.io to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your Public Key, Private Key, and Store Hash in Stamped.io.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your Public Key, Private Key, and Store Hash in Stamped.io\n\nTo obtain your Public Key, Private Key and Store Hash from your Stamped.io account:\n\nLog in to your Stamped.io account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Settings\n\nIn the left sidebar, click API Keys.\n\nClick + Add API Key to create a private key.\n\nCopy the API Public Key, Store Hash and API Private Key values shown and store them in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this values in the Public Key, Private Key and Store Hash fields in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Stamped.io in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Stamped.io module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Stamped.io modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Stamped.io Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nAction\n\nSearch Reviews\n\nPublish/Unpublish a Review\n\nCreate a Review\n\nOther\n\nWatch Reviews\n\nMake an API Call\n\nNote\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nWhen you create a Stamped.io webhook in Make, it is attached automatically and requires no additional set up.\n\nStamped.io\nConnect Stamped.io to Make\nObtain your Public Key, Private Key, and Store Hash in Stamped.io\nEstablish the connection with Stamped.io in Make\nBuild Stamped.io Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at sendsms.ro.\n\nRefer to the sendSMS API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect sendSMS to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in sendSMS.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in sendSMS\n\nTo obtain your API key from your sendSMS account:\n\nLog in to your sendSMS account.\n\nClick Account > API Keys.\n\nClick Generate a new API Key.\n\nIn the Description field, enter a description for your API key.\n\nClick Generate.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the Password/API key field in Make.\n\nNote\n\nAt the time of this publication, all steps for Obtain your API key in sendSMS were checked and verified to be accurate. However this may have changed, so please see the sendSMS API Key documentation or the sendSMS API key video for the most up-to-date directions.\n\nEstablish the connection with sendSMS in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a sendSMS module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Login name field, enter your sendSMS login name, which is also called Username on their login page.\n\nIn the Password/API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more sendSMS modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild sendSMS Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nSMS\n\nSend an SMS - GDPR\n\nGet Message Statuses\n\nSend an SMS\n\nContacts\n\nDelete a Contact\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nGet Contacts\n\nAdd a Contact\n\nGroups\n\nGet Groups\n\nAdd a Group\n\nDelete a Group\n\nBlock List\n\nAdd to Block List\n\nDelete from Block List\n\nBlock List Check\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nsendSMS\nConnect sendSMS to Make\nObtain your API key in sendSMS\nEstablish the connection with sendSMS in Make\nBuild sendSMS Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a Short.io account at app.short.cm/public/register.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Short.io to Make\n\nTo connect your Short.io account to Make you need to obtain the API key from your Short.io account.\n\nLog in to your Short.io account.\n\nOpen the menu in the top-left corner and select the Integrations & API option.\n\nCopy the provided Secret key by clicking on the copy icon next to the blurred key.\n\nGo to Make and open the Short.io module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nEnter the API Key you have copied in step 3 to the respective field and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nDomain\nWatch Domains\nList Domains\nLink\nGet Link\nCreate Link\nUpdate Link\nArchive Link\nExpire Link\nDelete Link\nMake an API Call\n\nAllows you to perform a custom API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Short.io account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.short.cm. E.g. links/expand\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Short.io API documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET\n\nto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST\n\nto create a new entry.\n\nPUT\n\nto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH\n\nto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE\n\nto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - Get Link Details by Domain and Path\n\nThe following API call returns link details:(see the Query String field. Domain and Path are the required parameters for this API call.)\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body.\n\nIn our example, these link details were returned:\n\nShort.io\nGetting Started with Short.io\nConnecting Short.io to Make\nDomain\nWatch Domains\nList Domains\nLink\nGet Link\nCreate Link\nUpdate Link\nArchive Link\nExpire Link\nDelete Link\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Link Details by Domain and Path\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a SendX account at app.sendx.io/register.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting SendX to Make\n\nTo connect your SendX account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your SendX account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your SendX account.\n\nClick Your Account Name > Settings.\n\nCopy the Team ID and API Key to a safe place.\n\nGo to Make and open the SendX module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Team ID and API Key fields, enter the team ID and API key details copied in step 3, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nContacts\nCreate / Update a Contact\nTags\nAdd a Tag to a Contact\nRemove a Tag from a Contact\nTriggers\nUniversal Trigger\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Identify a Contact\nSetting Up the SendX Webhooks\n\nOpen the Universal Trigger module, establish a connection, click Save and copy the URL address to your clipboard. Click OK and save the trigger.\n\nLog in to your SendX account. Click Automation > Create New Automation.\n\nIn the Trigger section, select the option, and its value for which you want to receive the trigger.\n\nIn the Action section, select Call Webhook, and add the URL address copied in step 1. Click Submit Automation.\n\nYou have successfully added the webhook to the SendX account.\n\nGo to Make and run the trigger. You will receive alerts for added triggers. For example, here you receive the triggers when a user subscribes to the Support list.\n\nSendX\nGetting Started with SendX\nConnecting SendX to Make\nContacts\nCreate / Update a Contact\nTags\nAdd a Tag to a Contact\nRemove a Tag from a Contact\nTriggers\nUniversal Trigger\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Identify a Contact\nSetting Up the SendX Webhooks\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Otevřete Make a dialog Create a connection SmartEmailing modulu.\n\n7. Zadejte do příslušných kolonek své uživatelské jméno a API klíč, který jste vygenerovali v kroku 5 výše a potvrďte kliknutím na Continue.\n\nSpojení bylo navázáno. If you do not have one, you can create a SendPulse account at sendpulse.com/register.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting SendPulse to Make\n\nTo connect your SendPulse account to Make you need to enable the REST API first.\n\nLog in to your SendPulse account.\n\nClick on your profile icon in the top-right corner and select the Account settings option.\n\nClick on the API tab, turn the Activate Rest API button on, and click the Save button.\n\nGo to Make and open the SendPulse module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the SendPulse website.\n\nEnter your credentials and click the Login button to establish the connection.n\n\nNote\n\nIf you do not have a password (if you have signed up using Google or Facebook) you must create one by clicking the Forgot password? link.\n\nContacts\nAdd a Contact\nList Contacts\nSearch a Contact by Variable\nSearch a Contact by Email\nGet a Contact\nUnsubscribe a Contact\nEmail/SMTP\nList Campaigns\nGet a Campaign\nSend an Email\nSend an Email from Template\nCreate a Template\nList Bounces\nPush\nList Website Subscriptions\nGet a Website\nActivate/deactivate a website subscriber\nCreate a Push Campaign\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Contacts From the Mailing List\nSendPulse\nGetting Started with SendPulse\nConnecting SendPulse to Make\nContacts\nAdd a Contact\nList Contacts\nSearch a Contact by Variable\nSearch a Contact by Email\nGet a Contact\nUnsubscribe a Contact\nEmail/SMTP\nList Campaigns\nGet a Campaign\nSend an Email\nSend an Email from Template\nCreate a Template\nList Bounces\nPush\nList Website Subscriptions\nGet a Website\nActivate/deactivate a website subscriber\nCreate a Push Campaign\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Contacts From the Mailing List\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingSendGrid\nSendGrid \nGetting started with SendGrid\n\nTo use any of the modules, you need to connect your SendGrid account to Make. If you do not have a SendGrid account yet, you can create one at SendGrid.com\n\nConnecting SendGrid to Make\n\nTo connect your SendGrid account to Make, follow the general instructions for connecting to any web service. When creating a scenario, you will be asked to provide an API Key. To get your API Key, log in to your SendGrid account and follow the instructions below.\n\n1. Go to Settings in the menu on the left, and open the API Keys dialog.\n\n2. Click on the Create API Key button in the top-right corner.\n\n3. Create the API Key with Full Access permissions.\n\n4. Copy the API Key to the clipboard and save it somewhere else.\n\n5. Paste the API Key to the API Key field in the Create a connection dialog of the desired module and click the Continue button.\n\n6. The connection is now established. You can continue creating your scenario.\n\nContacts (New)\nWatch Contacts (New)\n\nReturns contact details when a new contact is created or an existing contact is updated.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nWatch\n\n\t\n\nCreate + Update\n\nTriggers when a contact is created or update.\n\nCreate\n\nTriggers when a contact is created.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of contacts Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nCreate a List (New)\n\nCreates a new contact list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for your new list.\n\nAdd or Update a Contact (New)\n\nThis module adds or updates a contact.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nList\n\n\t\n\nSelect the lists you want to add the contact to.\n\n\n\n\nEmail address\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email address of the new contact or the contact you want to update.\n\nCaution\n\nIf the contact with the entered email address is found, it will be updated.\n\n\n\n\nFirst name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the new/updated recipient's first name.\n\n\n\n\nLast name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the new/updated recipient's last name.\n\n\n\n\nAlternate Emails\n\n\t\n\nAdd at most 5 additional email addresses.\n\n\n\n\nAddress Line 1\n\n\t\n\nEnter the first lines of the address.\n\n\n\n\nAddress Line 2\n\n\t\n\nEnter the second, optional, line of the address.\n\n\n\n\nCity\n\n\t\n\nEnter the city of the contact.\n\n\n\n\nState Province Region\n\n\t\n\nEnter the state, province, or region of the contact's address.\n\n\n\n\nPostal code\n\n\t\n\nEnter the postal code, Eircode, PIN code or ZIP code of the contact's address.\n\n\n\n\nCountry\n\n\t\n\nEnter the country of the contacts address. It can be full name or abbreviation.\n\n\n\n\nPhone number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the contact's phone number.\n\n\n\n\nWhatsapp\n\n\t\n\nEnter a Whatsapp account of the contact.\n\n\n\n\nLine\n\n\t\n\nEnter the landline phone number.\n\n\n\n\nFacebook\n\n\t\n\nEnter the contact's Facebook address.\n\n\n\n\nUnique Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the unique name for the contact.\n\n\n\n\nContact ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter or select the contact whose email you want to update.\n\nGet All Lists (New)\n\nThe module retrieves all of your contact lists.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nNumber of lists\n\n\t\n\nSet the number of returned contact lists.\n\nGet All Contacts (New)\n\nRetrieves all of your marketing campaigns' contacts.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nNumber of contacts to return\n\n\t\n\nSet the number of returned contacts.\n\nDelete a List (New)\n\nDeletes the list and optionally also deletes contacts associated with the list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nMap or select the list you want to delete.\n\n\n\n\nDelete Contacts\n\n\t\n\nEnable this option to also delete the contacts that are in the list you want to delete.\n\nDelete Contacts (New)\n\nDeletes specified contacts or all contacts at once.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nDelete all or Specific contacts\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to specify the contact(s) to be deleted or delete all contacts.\n\n\n\n\nContact IDs\n\n\t\n\nAdd (and map) IDs of contacts you want to delete.\n\n\n\n\nDelete All Contacts\n\n\t\n\nEnable this option to delete all contacts.\n\nRemove Contacts from a List (New)\n\nRemoves contacts from the specified list. It does not delete the contact.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nMap or select the list you want to remove the contact(s) from.\n\n\n\n\nContact IDs\n\n\t\n\nAdd the IDs of contacts you want to remove from the list.\n\nContacts (Legacy)\nNote\n\nLegacy modules are for users, who started to use these SendGrid modules before July 2019. Legacy modules do not work for new users as they don't have the required scopes within the API key.\n\nWatch New Lists (Legacy)\n\nWhen a new list is created, the List ID, Name, and Recipient Count are returned.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of lists Make will work with during one execution cycle.\n\nWatch New Recipients (Legacy)\n\nRetrieves contact details when a new contact is created in the selected list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the list you want to watch for new recipients.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of lists Make will work with during one execution cycle.\n\nCreate a List (Legacy)\n\nThis module allows you to create a list for your contacts.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for your new list.\n\nAdd or Update Recipient (Legacy)\n\nThis module adds or updates a Marketing Campaign's contact.\n\nThe rate limit is three requests every 2 seconds. You can upload 1000 contacts per request. So the maximum upload rate is 1500 recipients per second.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail address\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email address of the new contact or the contact you want to update.\n\nIf the contact with the entered email address is found, it will be updated.\n\n\n\n\nFirst name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the new/updated recipient's first name.\n\n\n\n\nLast name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the new/updated recipient's last name.\n\nAdd Recipients to a List (Legacy)\n\nAdds a contact to a list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (select from the drop-down menu or map) the ID of the list you want to add the contact to. The List ID can be retrieved, for example, using the Get All Lists search module.\n\n\n\n\nRecipients\n\n\t\n\nAdd (select from the drop-down menu or map) the contacts you want to add to the list. The Recipient ID can be retrieved, for example, using the Get All Recipients search module.\n\nGet All Lists (Legacy)\n\nThe module retrieves all of your contact lists.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nNumber of lists\n\n\t\n\nSet the number of returned contact lists.\n\nGet All Recipients (Legacy)\n\nRetrieves all of your marketing campaigns' contacts.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the list you want to retrieve recipients from.\n\n\n\n\nNumber of recipients\n\n\t\n\nSet the number of returned contacts.\n\nDelete a List (Legacy)\n\nDeletes a contact list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nLists\n\n\t\n\nAdd the IDs of the list(s) you want to delete. The List ID can be retrieved, for example, using the Get All Lists search module.\n\nDelete Recipients (Legacy)\n\nThis module allows you to delete one or more recipients.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nRecipients\n\n\t\n\nSelect the recipient you want to delete.\n\nDelete Recipients from a List (Legacy)\n\nDeletes recipient from a selected list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the list you want to delete the recipient from.\n\n\n\n\nRecipient ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the recipient or enter (map) the ID of the recipient you want to delete from the list.\n\nBounces\nGet All Bounces\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nStart time\n\n\t\n\nSet the start of the time range when a bounce was created (inclusive).\n\n\n\n\nEnd time\n\n\t\n\nSet the end of the time range when a bounce was created (inclusive).\n\n\n\n\nNumber of bounces\n\n\t\n\nSet the number of returned bounces.\n\nDelete Bounces\n\nRemoves a specific email address from your bounce list.\n\nA bounced email is when the message is undeliverable and then returned to the server that sent it.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nEmails\n\n\t\n\nAdd the emails you want to remove from the Bounces list.\n\nDelete All Bounces\n\nDeletes all email addresses from the bounce list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\nBlocks\n\nThere are several causes for blocked emails, for example: your mail server IP address is on an ISP blacklist or blocked by an ISP, or if the receiving server flags the message content.\n\nList Blocks\n\nRetrieves all email addresses that are currently on your block list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nStart Time\n\n\t\n\nEnter the start date and time of the range when a blocked email was created (inclusive).\n\n\n\n\nEnd Time\n\n\t\n\nEnter the end date and time of the range when a blocked email was created (inclusive).\n\n\n\n\nNumber of blocked emails to return\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of email addresses Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nGet a Block\n\nRetrieves block details.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail address\n\n\t\n\nEnter the blocked email address you want to retrieve details about.\n\nDelete Blocks\n\nRemoves all or specified emails from the block list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nDelete All or Specific\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to delete all or specific emails.\n\nIf the Delete Specific Emails option is selected, specify email addresses you want to delete in the Email address field below.\n\nGlobal Suppressions\nList Global Suppressions\n\nReturns all globally suppressed email addresses.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nStart Time\n\n\t\n\nEnter the start date and time of the range when a suppressed email was created (inclusive).\n\n\n\n\nEnd Time\n\n\t\n\nEnter the end date and time of the range when a suppressed email was created (inclusive).\n\n\n\n\nNumber of emails to return\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of email addresses Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nGet a Global Suppression\n\nChecks whether a specified email belongs to global suppressions.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email you want to check.\n\nAdd Emails to Global Suppression\n\nAdds email addresses to the global suppressions.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nRecipient Emails\n\n\t\n\nEnter the emails you want to add to global unsubscribes.\n\nDelete a Global Suppression\n\nRemoves an email from global suppressions.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email you want to delete from global unsubscribes.\n\nOther\nSend an Email\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nFrom\n\n\t\n\nEmail Address\n\nEnter the email address of the sender.\n\nName\n\nEnter the name of the sender.\n\n\n\n\nSend to\n\n\t\n\nAdd recipient email addresses. The maximum number of email addresses is 1000.\n\n\n\n\nUse SendGrid Transactional template?\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to use the SendGrid template or not.\n\nIf you select Yes, the Template ID must be provided. You can retrieve the Template ID via SendGrid - Templates - Transactional.\n\n\n\n\nMap JSON or fill Keys and Values\n\n\t\n\nEnables you to enter data in the template dynamically.\n\nSelect whether you want to specify data using JSON or by entering Key and Value pairs.\n\n\n\n\nDynamic Template Data\n\n\t\n\nEnter JSON or define key and value pairs.\n\nFor more information about specifying dynamic template data please refer to the Using Handlebars documentation.\n\n\n\n\nSubject\n\n\t\n\nEnter the subject for the email.\n\n\n\n\nContent type\n\n\t\n\nSelect the MIME type of the email content.\n\n\n\n\nContent\n\n\t\n\nEnter the content of the email you want to send.\n\n\n\n\nAttachments\n\n\t\n\nAdd the file(s) you want to attach. For inline images enter the Content ID.\n\n\n\n\nSend at\n\n\t\n\nEnter the time and date when the email should be sent.\n\nScheduling more than 72 hours in advance is not allowed.\n\n\n\n\nCopy recipient\n\n\t\n\nEnter the copy recipient(s). CC - carbon copy. The maximum is 999 recipients.\n\n\n\n\nBlind copy recipient\n\n\t\n\nEnter the blind copy recipient(s). BCC - blind carbon copy. The maximum is 999 recipients.\n\n\n\n\nReply To\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email address and name that will be used for the email reply.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nAdd custom headers if needed.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nAllows you to perform a custom API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your SendGrid account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.sendgrid.com/v3/. E.g. /marketing/contacts\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Sendgrid API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET: to retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST: to create a new entry.\n\nPUT: to update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH: to make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE: to delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Contacts\n\nThe following API call returns all marketing contacts in your Sendgrid account:\n\nURL:\n\n/marketing/contacts\n\nMethod:\n\nGET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > result.\n\nIn our example, 3 contacts were returned:\n\nSendGrid\nGetting started with SendGrid\nConnecting SendGrid to Make\nContacts (New)\nWatch Contacts (New)\nCreate a List (New)\nAdd or Update a Contact (New)\nGet All Lists (New)\nGet All Contacts (New)\nDelete a List (New)\nDelete Contacts (New)\nRemove Contacts from a List (New)\nContacts (Legacy)\nWatch New Lists (Legacy)\nWatch New Recipients (Legacy)\nCreate a List (Legacy)\nAdd or Update Recipient (Legacy)\nAdd Recipients to a List (Legacy)\nGet All Lists (Legacy)\nGet All Recipients (Legacy)\nDelete a List (Legacy)\nDelete Recipients (Legacy)\nDelete Recipients from a List (Legacy)\nBounces\nGet All Bounces\nDelete Bounces\nDelete All Bounces\nBlocks\nList Blocks\nGet a Block\nDelete Blocks\nGlobal Suppressions\nList Global Suppressions\nGet a Global Suppression\nAdd Emails to Global Suppression\nDelete a Global Suppression\nOther\nSend an Email\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Contacts\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at sendlane.com.\n\nRefer to the Sendlane API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Sendlane to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Sendlane module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Email and Password fields, enter your Sendlane account credentials.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, you must:\n\nObtain your webhook URL in Make.\n\nConfigure a webhook trigger in Sendlane.\n\nObtain your webhook URL in Make\n\nAdd an Sendlane instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nYou will use this value in Sendlane.\n\nConfigure a webhook trigger in Sendlane\n\nLog in to your Sendlane account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Automations.\n\nClick New Automation and Start from Scratch or choose a template automation in the Our Automations section.\n\nEnter a name and click Start.\n\nClick the plus icon under the Add trigger action and click Webhook in the left sidebar.\n\nIn the URL field, paste the webhook URL copied in step 4.\n\nIn the method dropdown menu, select GET and click Done.\n\nSendlane will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild Sendlane Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nSubscriptions\n\nAdd a Contact\n\nUnsubscribe a Contact\n\nTriggers\n\nWatch Automation\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nSendlane\nConnect Sendlane to Make\nSet Up Sendlane Webhooks\nObtain your webhook URL in Make\nConfigure a webhook trigger in Sendlane\nBuild Sendlane Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a Platformly account at www.platform.ly.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Platformly to Make\n\nTo connect your Platformly account to Make you need to add a new API Key to your Platformly account and insert the created API Key to the Make Platformly module connection dialog.\n\nLog in to your Platformly account and open the API Docs & Keys settings.\n\nClick on the New API Key button.\n\nEnter the name for the API Key, copy the provided API Key and click on the Submit button.\n\nGo to Make and open the Create a connection dialog in the desired module. Enter the API Key into the respective field.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button you can proceed to set up the Platformly module.\n\nTriggers\nWatch Contacts\nActions\nAdd a Contact\nUpdate a Contact\nAdd a Tag\nRemove a Tag\nRemove All Tags\nAdd a Note\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Contacts\nSearches\nGet a Contact\nList Contacts\nPlatformly\nGetting Started with Platformly\nConnecting Platformly to Make\nTriggers\nWatch Contacts\nActions\nAdd a Contact\nUpdate a Contact\nAdd a Tag\nRemove a Tag\nRemove All Tags\nAdd a Note\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Contacts\nSearches\nGet a Contact\nList Contacts\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at producthunt.com.\n\nRefer to the Product Hunt API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Product Hunt to Make\n\nTo connect your Product Hunt account to Make, you must first create a custom app in your Product Hunt account and obtain your custom app credentials.\n\nLog in to your Product Hunt account.\n\nIn the top-right corner, hover over your account icon and click on the API dashboard option.\n\nClick on the Add an application button.\n\nEnter a Name for your application (for example, Make) and paste the following address in the Redirect URI field: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/product-hunt.\n\nClick on the Create Application button.\n\nCopy the API Key and API Secret values and store them in a safe place. You will use these values in the Client ID and Client Secret fields when establishing the connection in Make.\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Product Hunt module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Client ID field, paste the API Key value copied in Step 6.\n\nIn the Client Secret field, paste the API Secret value copied in Step 6.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Product Hunt modules. Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingMautic\nMautic\n\nThe Mautic modules enable you to monitor events, search, retrieve, create, update, or delete contacts, companies, segments, and stages in your account.\n\nTo get started with Mautic, create an account at mautic.org.\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Mautic API Documentation.\n\nConnecting Mautic to Make\n\nTo connect your Mautic account to Make you need to enable the API in your Mautic account and obtain your Domain, Client ID and Client Secret.\n\nEnabling API\n\nLog in to your Mautic account.\n\nGo to Settings > Configuration.\n\nOpen API Settings and switch API enabled? option to Yes and save the dialog by clicking the Apply or Save & Close button.\n\nRetrieving API Credentials\n\nLog in to your Mautic account.\n\nGo to Settings > API Credentials.\n\nClick the +New button.\n\nFill in the dialog fields as follows:\n\nAuthorization Protocol\n\n\t\n\nOAuth 2\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired name, for example: Make\n\n\n\n\nRedirect URI\n\n\t\n\nhttps://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/mautic\n\nClick the Save & Close button.\n\nFind the Client ID (Public Key) and Client Secret on the API Credentials page.\n\nGo to Make and open the Mautic module's Create a Connection dialog.\n\nEnter the Client ID and Client Secret you have retrieved in Step 7 to the respective fields and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the Mautic website, where you will be prompted to grant Make access to your account.\n\nConfirm the dialog by clicking the Accept button.\n\nThe connection has been established. You can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nBuild Mautic Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nWatch Events\n\nTriggers when a new event given by the selection parameter is occured.\n\nCreate/Update a Contact\n\nCreate a new contact. If the contact with the same e-mail already exists, it is updated.\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nUpdates an existing contact.\n\nGet a Contact\n\nGets an individual contact by ID.\n\nSearch Contacts\n\nRetrieves a list of contacts by a search.\n\nDelete a Contact\n\nDeletes a contact.\n\nCreates/Update a Company\n\nCreates a new company. If the company with the same company's name already exists, it is updated.\n\nUpdate a Company\n\nUpdates an existing company.\n\nGet a Company\n\nGets an individual company by ID.\n\nList Companies\n\nReturns a list of all companies available to the user.\n\nDelete a Company\n\nDeletes a company.\n\nCreate a Stage\n\nCreates a new stage.\n\nUpdate a Stage\n\nUpdates an existing stage.\n\nAdd Contact to a Stage\n\nAdds a contact to a specific stage.\n\nRemove Contact from a Stage\n\nRemoves contact from a specific stage.\n\nGet a Stage\n\nGets an individual stage by ID.\n\nList Stages\n\nReturns a list of all contact stages.\n\nDelete a Stage\n\nDeletes a stage.\n\nCreate a Segment\n\nCreates a new segment.\n\nUpdate a Segment\n\nUpdates an existing segment.\n\nAdd Contact to a Segment\n\nAdds a contact to a specific segment.\n\nAdd Contact to a Segment\n\nAdds a contact to a specific segment.\n\nRemove Contact from a Segment\n\nRemoves contact from a specific segment.\n\nGet a Segment\n\nGets an individual segment by ID.\n\nList Segments\n\nReturns a list of all segments.\n\nDelete a Segment\n\nDeletes a segment.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nMautic\nConnecting Mautic to Make\nEnabling API\nRetrieving API Credentials\nBuild Mautic Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Some of the mandatory fields are listed below:\n\nClient name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the application. For example, Make\n\n\n\n\nApplication Website\n\n\t\n\nA link to your application's public home page. For example, https://www.make.com.\n\n\n\n\nRedirect URL\n\n\t\n\nhttps://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/meetup\n\nCopy the Key and Secret values to a safe place.\n\nGo to Make, and open the Meetup Pro module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nEnter the Client ID and Client Secret from step 4 to the respective fields, and click the Save.\n\nThe connection has been established. You can create an account at memberful.com.\n\nRefer to the Memberful API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nSet Up Memberful Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd an Memberful instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nLog in to your Memberful account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Settings.\n\nIn the Integrate section, click Webhooks.\n\nClick Add a new webhook.\n\nEnter a Name for the webhook.\n\nIn the Endpoint URL field, paste the webhook URL copied in Step 3.\n\nIn the Select events to listen to section, select the event to watch for, corresponding to the Memberful module you added in Make.\n\nMemberful will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild Memberful Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nMembers\n\nWatch Member Signup\n\nWatch Member Updated\n\nWatch Member Deleted\n\nSubscriptions\n\nWatch Subscription Created\n\nWatch Subscription Updated\n\nWatch Subscription Renewed\n\nWatch Subscription Activated\n\nWatch Subscription Deactivated\n\nWatch Subscription Deleted\n\nOrders\n\nWatch Order Purchased\n\nWatch Order Refunded\n\nWatch Order Suspended\n\nWatch Order Completed\n\nMemberful\nSet Up Memberful Webhooks\nBuild Memberful Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, create an account at https://manage.mailmodo.com/auth/signup.\n\nFor more information about Integration and APIs in Mailmodo, go to Mailmodo support articles.\n\nConnect Mailmodo to Make\n\nTo connect your Maimodo account to Make, you need first get the API Key from your Mailmodo account.\n\nLog in to your Mailmodo account and go to Integrations from the vertical menu on the left.\n\nUnder Available for Connection, locate Make and click the authentication CTA.\n\nFrom the Make Integration window, copy the API key value shown. You will enter this value in Make to establish the connection.\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Mailmodo module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied in Step 3.\n\nClick Save.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Mailmodo modules.\n\nBuild Mailmodo Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nTriggers\n\nWatch Submissions\n\nActions\n\nAdd to Contact List\n\nNote: This module allows you to add or update contacts in a Mailmodo list whenever an event is recorded in the trigger app. For example, whenever a new contact is added to the Google sheet, it will automatically be imported into a Mailmodo list.\n\nTrigger Campaign\n\nNote: This module allows you to automatically send a campaign to a contact in Mailmodo whenever an event is logged in the trigger app. For example, whenever a new email address is added to the Google sheet, a campaign will be triggered and sent to the corresponding contact. For more details, check out how to trigger campaigns in Mailmodo via Make.\n\nTrigger Journey\n\nNote: This module allows you to automatically enroll contacts into a journey in Mailmodo whenever an event is recorded in the trigger app. For example, whenever a new email address is added to the Google sheet, we will automatically enroll the contact into a journey in Mailmodo. For more details, check out how to trigger journeys in Mailmodo via Make.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nNote\n\nTo learn how to create a scenario in Make using Mailmodo and Google Sheet as the trigger app, you can find step-by-step instructions here.\n\nMailmodo\nConnect Mailmodo to Make\nBuild Mailmodo Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

22, 2022, new users will be unable to use the v2 API.\n\nThe MailerLite Classic supports only the API v1.\n\nFor more information regarding the MailerLite Classic and new MailerLite versions, see the MailerLite vs MailerLite Classic documentation.\n\nWith the MailerLite Classic modules in Make, you can:\n\nwatch, list, create, execute the campaign actions, upload the campaign content, and remove campaigns\n\nwatch, search, retrieve, list, add, and update subscribers\n\nlist, retrieve, create, update, and remove groups\n\nlist and retrieve the group subscribers, remove subscribers from the group, and list group subscribers by type\n\ncall APIs\n\nTo get started with the MailerLite app, create an account at Mailerlite.com.\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the MailerLite Classic API documentation.\n\nConnect MailerLite Classic to Make\n\nTo connect the MailerLite Classic app with the Make:\n\nLog in to your MailerLite account.\n\nChoose the app you want to connect to.\n\nMailerLite Classic: supports only API v1.\n\nMailerLite: supports both API v1 and v2.\n\nClick your account name in the left side panel and select Integrations.\n\nFrom the list of integrations, choose Developer API > Use.\n\nClick New, enter a name for the new API token and click Create token.\n\nNow copy the API key to a safe place.\n\nLog in to your Make and add a MailerLite Classic module into a Make scenario.\n\nClick Add next to the Connection field.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the details copied in step 5 and click Save.\n\nYou have successfully connected the MailerLite Classic app with Make and can now build and run your scenario.\n\nBuild MailerLite Classic Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nWatch Campaigns\n\nRuns when a new company is added to your account.\n\nList Campaigns\n\nLists all campaigns by status.\n\nCreate Campaign\n\nCreates a campaign where you will use your custom HTML template.\n\nExecute Campaign Action\n\nSends, schedules, or cancels campaigns.\n\nUpload Campaign Content\n\nUploads your HTML template to a created campaign.\n\nRemove Campaign\n\nRemoves a campaign.\n\nWatch Subscribers\n\nTriggers when an event occurs to subscribers.\n\nSearch Subscribers By Email\n\nSearches for subscribers by email.\n\nGet Subscriber\n\nGets a single subscriber by OD or email address.\n\nList Subscriber Activity\n\nLists activity (clicks, opens, etc.) of selected subscribers.\n\nList Subscriber Activity by Type\n\nLists activity of selected subscribers by specified type (opens, clicks, etc.)\n\nAdd Subscriber to a Group\n\nAdds a new single subscriber to a specified group.\n\nUpdate Subscriber\n\nUpdates single subscriber by ID or Email.\n\nList Groups\n\nLists all groups for this account.\n\nList Subscriber Groups\n\nLists group subscriber belongs to.\n\nGet You can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nWebinars/Events\nWatch Webinars Start\nWatch Webinars Published\nWatch Webinars End\nSearch Events\nPeople\nWatch New Registrants\nSearch People\nGet a Person\nCreate a Registrant\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Events\nLivestorm\nGetting Started with Livestorm\nConnecting Livestorm to Make\nWebinars/Events\nWatch Webinars Start\nWatch Webinars Published\nWatch Webinars End\nSearch Events\nPeople\nWatch New Registrants\nSearch People\nGet a Person\nCreate a Registrant\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Events\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can associate a conversion to a campaign, and generate offline conversion reports.\n\nGetting Started with LinkedIn Offline Conversions\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA LinkedIn account: create an account at linkedin.com/signup\n\nUser permissions: rw_offlineConversions, rw_ads, r_ads_reporting\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting LinkedIn Offline Conversions with Make\n\nLog in to your Make account.\n\nAdd a module from the LinkedIn Offline Conversions app into a Make scenario.\n\nClick Add next to the Connection field.\n\nClick Save and enter your LinkedIn account credentials.\n\nConfirm the access by clicking Allow.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nActions\nCreate an offline Conversion Segment\n\nCreates a new offline conversion segment.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nAccount\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account for which you want to create the offline conversion segment.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a name for the segment.\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the details of the segment.\n\nSend Offline Conversion Events\n\nSends multiple offline conversion events in a batch.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nAccount URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account to which you want to send the offline conversion events\n\n\n\n\nSegment ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Segment ID used for conversion events.\n\n\n\n\nEvents\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the event details. You can add multiple actions.\n\nAction\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the action you want to perform:\n\nAdd\n\nRemove\n\n\n\n\nUser\n\n\t\n\nEnter the user details:\n\nUser IDs\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the user's email address. You can add multiple email addresses by clicking Add item.\n\n\n\n\nFirst Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the user's first name. The maximum number of allowed characters is 35.\n\n\n\n\nLast Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the user's last name. The maximum number of allowed characters is 35.\n\n\n\n\nTitle\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the user's job title. The maximum number of allowed characters is 50.\n\n\n\n\nCompany\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the user's company name. The maximum number of allowed characters is 50.\n\n\n\n\nCountry\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the user's country. Enter a two-letter country code. For example, US.\n\n\n\n\nConversion\n\n\t\n\nEnter the conversion details:\n\nConversion Happened At\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the time at which the conversion happened. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nConversion Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the conversion type. For example, download.\n\n\n\n\nMoney Amount\n\n\t\n\nEnter the amount details.\n\nAmount\n\nEnter the amount applicable to the conversion.\n\nCurrency\n\nEnter the applicable three-letter currency code.\n\nCreate a Conversion Rule\n\nCreates a new conversion rule to track offline conversions.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nAccount URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account for which you want to create the conversion rule.\n\n\n\n\nSegment URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the segment to create the conversion rule.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a name for the conversion rule.\n\n\n\n\nType\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the offline conversion rule type to track this conversion rule. For example, Ad Click. See the complete list of conversion rule types.\n\n\n\n\nAttribution Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the attribution type that describes the process to count the conversion actions:\n\nLast touch by campaign\n\nLast touch by conversion\n\n\n\n\nPost Click Attribution Window Size\n\n\t\n\nSpecifies a user's settings on the post-click attribution window in days. For example, 5.\n\n\n\n\nView through Attribution Window Size\n\n\t\n\nSpecifies a user's settings on the view through (post view) attribution window in days. For example, 5.\n\nAssociate Campaign to Conversion\n\nAssociates a campaign to a conversion rule by their IDs.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Campaign ID which you want to associate with the conversion.\n\n\n\n\nConversion Rule ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Conversion Rule ID to which you want to associate the campaign.\n\nGet an Offline Conversion Segment\n\nRetrieves the details of an offline conversion segment by its ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nSegment ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Segment ID whose details you want to retrieve.\n\nSearches\nGenerate an Offline Conversion Report\n\nGenerates an offline conversion report.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the accounts for which you want to generate the offline conversion report.\n\n\n\n\nTime Granularity\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the time for which you want to generate the report:\n\nAll\n\nDaily\n\nMonthly\n\nYearly\n\n\n\n\nStart Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the date to generate the report of the offline conversions that occurred on or after the specified date. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nEnd Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the date to generate the report of the offline conversions that occurred on or before the specified date. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nPivots\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the pivots to include in the report. Conversion is the default pivot and you can add at the most two additional pivots to include in the report.\n\n\n\n\nFields\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the fields to include in the report:\n\nExternal Website Conversion\n\nExternal Website Post Click Conversion\n\nExternal Website Post View Conversion\n\nViral External Website Conversion\n\nViral External Website Post Click Conversion\n\nViral External Website Post View Conversion\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the campaign type for which you want to generate the report:\n\nText Ad\n\nSponsored Updates\n\nSponsored InMails\n\nDynamic\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of results Make should return during one execution cycle.\n\nList Conversion Rules\n\nRetrieves a list of conversion rules by the ad account.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nAccount URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose conversion rules you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of conversion rules Make should return during one execution cycle.\n\nList Offline Conversion Segments\n\nRetrieves a list of offline conversion segments and filters by criteria.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Offline Conversions account.\n\n\n\n\nAccount\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose offline conversion segments you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nIs from Integromat\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to list only the offline conversion segments created from Integromat.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of offline conversion segments Make should return during one execution cycle.\n\nGetting Started with LinkedIn Offline Conversions\nConnecting LinkedIn Offline Conversions with Make\nActions\nCreate an offline Conversion Segment\nSend Offline Conversion Events\nCreate a Conversion Rule\nAssociate Campaign to Conversion\nGet an Offline Conversion Segment\nSearches\nGenerate an Offline Conversion Report\nList Conversion Rules\nList Offline Conversion Segments\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."
