Retrieve member’s advertising accounts\n\nrw_dmp_segments - Create and manage member’s matched audiences\n\nYou can create an account at linkedin.com\n\nRefer to the LinkedIn API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect LinkedIn Matched Audiences to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a LinkedIn Matched Audiences module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom app client credentials. For more information, refer to LinkedIn documentation.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/linkedin2\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more LinkedIn Matched Audiences modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild LinkedIn Matched Audiences Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nAudience\n\nSearch Audiences\n\nCreate an Audience\n\nGet An Audience\n\nDelete an Audience\n\nUsers\n\nAdd Users\n\nRemove Users\n\nCompany\n\nAdd Companies\n\nRemove Companies\n\nList\n\nCreate a List Upload Audience\n\nUpload a List File\n\nAttach a List File\n\nConnect LinkedIn Matched Audiences to Make\nBuild LinkedIn Matched Audiences Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingLinkedIn Lead Gen Forms\nLinkedIn Lead Gen Forms\n\nWith the LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms modules in Make you can:\n\nList, create, retrieve, and update the form and form status\n\nWatch, list, retrieve, and deregister the form responses\n\nTo get started with the LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms create an account at  linkedin.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnect LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms to Make\n\nLog in to your Make account.\n\nAdd a module from the LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms app into a Make scenario.\n\nClick Add next to the Connection field.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection and click Save.\n\nIn the Email and Password fields, enter your LinkedIn account credentials and click Sign in.\n\nConfirm the access by clicking Allow.\n\nYou have successfully connected LinkedIn Lead Gen Form app with Make and can now build scenarios.\n\nForm\n\nYou can create, update, list, retrieve the forms, and form status\n\nList Forms\n\nRetrieves a list of Lead Gen Forms.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nAd Account URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose forms you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of forms Make will return during one scenario execution cycle. The default value is 10.\n\nCreate a Form\n\nCreates a new Lead Gen Form.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nAd Account URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account for which you want to create the form.\n\n\n\n\nLanguage\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map a language in which you want to create the form.\n\n\n\n\nForm\n\n\t\n\nEnter the form details:\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a name for the form. The maximum number of allowed characters is 256 characters.\n\n\n\n\nHeadline\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the headline for the form. The maximum number of allowed characters is 60.\n\n\n\n\nPrivacy Policy URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the privacy policy URL address applicable to the form.\n\n\n\n\nLead Profile Information\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the lead profile information.\n\nNote\n\nAt least one custom question is required. A maximum of 12 questions in total are allowed.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Questions\n\n\t\n\nEnter the questions to add to the form. You can add multiple questions.\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the form details. The maximum number of allowed characters is 160.\n\n\n\n\nLegal Disclaimer\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the legal disclaimer content. The maximum number of allowed characters is 2000.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Checkboxes\n\n\t\n\nEnter the consent details for the form that are presented to the user:\n\nContent\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the consent text to display to the viewer. For example, this is a required checkbox. The maximum number of characters allowed is 500.\n\n\n\n\nConsent Required\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the consent is mandatory.\n\n\n\n\nThank You Message\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the thank you message that appears when a user completes the form. The maximum number of allowed characters is 300.\n\n\n\n\nLanding Page URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the form's landing page URL address to the user who is redirected after submitting the form.\n\n\n\n\nThank You Message Call-to-action\n\n\t\n\nSelect the text that appears on the call to action button after the user submits the form:\n\nVisit company website\n\nLearn More\n\nView Now\n\nDownload Now\n\nTry Now\n\n\n\n\nHidden Fields\n\n\t\n\nAdd the hidden fields for tracking user attributes. You can add a maximum of 20 fields.\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the field name.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the field value.\n\nGet a Form\n\nRetrieves the details of a Lead Gen Form.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nForm ID or URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Form ID or URN whose details you want to retrieve the form. Alternatively, you can search for the form.\n\nUpdate a Form\n\nUpdates an existing Lead Gen Form by its ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nForm ID or URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Form ID or account URN whose details you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nForm\n\n\t\n\nEnter the form details to update:\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a new name for the form. The maximum number of allowed characters is 256.\n\n\n\n\nHeadline\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a new headline for the form. The maximum number of allowed characters is 60.\n\n\n\n\nPrivacy Policy URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the privacy policy URL address that covers any data passed to the owner of the form.\n\n\n\n\nLead Profile Information\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the lead profile information.\n\nNote\n\nAt least one custom question is required.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Questions\n\n\t\n\nEnter the questions to add to the form. You can add multiple questions.\n\n\n\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the form details. The maximum number of allowed characters is 160.\n\n\n\n\nLegal Disclaimer\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the legal disclaimer content. The maximum number of allowed characters is 2000.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Checkboxes\n\n\t\n\nEnter the consent details for the form that are presented to the user:\n\nContent\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the consent text to display to the viewer. For example, this is a required checkbox. The maximum number of characters allowed is 500.\n\n\n\n\nConsent Required\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the consent is mandatory.\n\n\n\n\nThank You Message\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the thank you message that appears when a user completes the form. The maximum number of allowed characters is 300.\n\n\n\n\nLanding Page URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the form's landing page URL address to the user who is redirected after submitting the form.\n\n\n\n\nThank You Message Call-to-action\n\n\t\n\nSelect the text that appears on the call to action button after the user submits the form:\n\nVisit company website\n\nLearn More\n\nView Now\n\nDownload Now\n\nTry Now\n\n\n\n\nHidden Fields\n\n\t\n\nAdd the hidden field names and their values for tracking user attributes. You can add a maximum of 20 fields.\n\nUpdate a Form Status\n\nUpdates the status of a Lead Gen Form by its ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nForm ID or URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Form ID or URN whose status you want to update. Alternatively, you can search for the form.\n\n\n\n\nStatus\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the form status to which you want to update:\n\nSubmitted\n\nPaused\n\nArchived\n\nCanceled\n\nGet a Form Question\n\nRetrieves the details of a question of a Lead Gen Form by its ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nForm ID or URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the Form ID or URN whose questions you want to retrieve. Alternatively, you can search for the form question.\n\n\n\n\nQuestion ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a Question ID whose details you want to retrieve.\n\nResponse\n\nYou can watch, list, and retrieve the form responses.\n\nWatch Form Responses\n\nTriggers when a Lead Gen Form is submitted.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nAd Account URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Ad Account URN whose form responses you want to watch.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the campaign URN to watch the form responses.\n\nWatch Form Responses\n\nTriggers when a Lead Gen Form is submitted.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nAd Account URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Ad Account URN whose form responses you want to watch.\n\n\n\n\nForm URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Form URN to watch the form responses.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a campaign URN. Alternatively, you can search the campaign URN.\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose responses you want to watch.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Groups\n\n\t\n\nAdd the campaign groups whose responses you want to watch.\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose campaign groups you want to select.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the campaign groups:\n\nActive\n\nArchive\n\nCanceled\n\nDraft\n\nPaused\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Names\n\n\t\n\nEnter or map the campaign names to search the campaign groups.\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign was a test.\n\n\n\n\nAssociated Entities\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) an associated entity to search the campaign group.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status of the campaign:\n\nActive\n\nPaused\n\nArchived\n\nCompleted\n\nCanceled\n\nDraft\n\n\n\n\nTypes\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the campaign type:\n\nText Ad\n\nSponsored Updates\n\nSponsored InMails\n\nDynamic\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Names\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the campaign names whose responses you want to watch.\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign was a test.\n\n\n\n\nCreative URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the creative URN. Alternatively, you can search for a creative URN.\n\nCampaigns\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a name for the campaign. You can also search for a campaign.\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose creative URN you want to select.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Groups\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the name of the campaign group. You can also search for a campaign group.\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose campaign groups you want to select.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the campaign groups:\n\nActive\n\nArchive\n\nCancelled\n\nDraft\n\nPaused\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Names\n\n\t\n\nEnter or map the campaign names to search the campaign groups.\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign was a test.\n\n\n\n\nAssociated Entities\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) an associated entity to search the campaign group.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the campaign groups:\n\nActive\n\nArchived\n\nCompleted\n\nCanceled\n\nDraft\n\n\n\n\nTypes\n\n\t\n\nTypes Select the type of campaign:\n\nText Ad\n\nSponsored Updates\n\nSponsored InMails\n\nDynamic\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Names\n\n\t\n\nEnter or map the campaign names to search the campaign groups.\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign was a test\n\n\n\n\nReferences\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a reference share URN to watch the form responses.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the campaign groups:\n\nActive\n\nPaused\n\nDraft\n\nArchive\n\nCanceled\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the creative URN is a test.\n\n\n\n\nFields\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) fields associated with your query. You can enter multiple values by separating them with a comma.\n\nNote\n\nSee for more information on fields.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nEnter the maximum number of results Makeshould return during one scenario execution cycle. The default value is 2.\n\nList Form Responses\n\nRetrieves a list of responses of a Lead Gen Form.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nAd Account URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Ad Account URN whose form responses you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nForm URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Form URN to list the form response.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a campaign URN. Alternatively, you can search for the campaign URN.\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose campaign groups you want to select.\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Groups\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the campaign groups. You can also search campaign groups.\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose campaign groups you want to select.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the campaign groups:\n\nActive\n\nArchive\n\nCanceled\n\nDraft\n\nPaused\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Names\n\n\t\n\nEnter or map the campaign names to search the campaign groups.\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign was a test.\n\n\n\n\nAssociated Entities\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) an associated entity to search the campaign group.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the campaign groups:\n\nActive\n\nPaused\n\nArchived\n\nCompleted\n\nCanceled\n\nDraft\n\n\n\n\nTypes\n\n\t\n\nTypes Select the type of campaign:\n\nText Ad\n\nSponsored Updates\n\nSponsored InMails\n\nDynamic\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Names\n\n\t\n\nEnter or map the campaign names to search the campaign groups.\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign is a test.\n\n\n\n\nCreative URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a creative URN to list the form response. You can also search for the creative URN.\n\nCampaign\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a campaign name to search for a creative URN.\n\nAccounts\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the account whose campaign groups you want to select.\n\n\n\n\nAssociated Entities\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) an associated entity to search the campaign group.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the campaign groups:\n\nActive\n\nPaused\n\nArchived\n\nCompleted\n\nCanceled\n\n\n\n\nTypes\n\n\t\n\nSelect the type of campaign:\n\nText Ad\n\nSponsored Updates\n\nSponsored InMails\n\nDynamic\n\n\n\n\nCampaign Names\n\n\t\n\nEnter or map the campaign names to search the campaign groups.\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign is a test.\n\n\n\n\nReference\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the reference share URN.\n\n\n\n\nStatuses\n\n\t\n\nSelect the status to search the creative URN:\n\nActive\n\nPaused\n\nDraft\n\nArchived\n\nCanceled\n\n\n\n\nIs Test\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the campaign was a test.\n\n\n\n\nStart Time\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the start date and time to list the form responses. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nEnd Time\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the end date and time up to which the form responses should be listed. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nEnter the maximum number of results Makeshould return during one scenario execution cycle. The default value is 10.\n\nGet a Form Responses\n\nRetrieves a response of a Lead Gen Form.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nAd Account URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map an Ad Account URN to retrieve form responses.\n\n\n\n\nResponse ID or URN\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) a response ID or URN to retrieve the form responses.\n\nDeregister a Form Response Webhook\n\nDeregisters an existing Lead Gen Form webhook by the entity ID.\n\nImportant\n\nThis module should only be used against the \"webhook already exist\" error. Use with extreme caution.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nAd Account URN\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map an Ad Account URN to deregister a form response webhook.\n\nOthers\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API Call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.linkedin.com/. For example, /v2/me.\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms API.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET\n\nto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST\n\nto create a new entry.\n\nPUT\n\nto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH\n\nto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE\n\nto delete an entry\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of use - List Forms\n\nThe following API call returns all the forms from your LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms account:\n\nURL:\n\n/v2/adForms/q=account&account=<accountid>\n\nMethod:\n\nGET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > elements. \n\nIn our example, 4 forms were returned:\n\nLinkedIn Lead Gen Forms\nConnect LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms to Make\nForm\nList Forms\nCreate a Form\nGet a Form\nUpdate a Form\nUpdate a Form Status\nGet a Form Question\nResponse\nWatch Form Responses\nWatch Form Responses\nList Form Responses\nGet a Form Responses\nDeregister a Form Response Webhook\nOthers\nMake an API Call\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Events\nLinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events\n\nWith LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events modules in Make, you can get and monitor your event forms.\n\nTo use the LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events modules, you must have a LinkedIn account. You can create an account at linkedin.com.\n\nRefer to the Lead Sync Forms API Documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events to Make\n\nTo establish the connection:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a LinkedIn Gen Forms - Event module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom app client credentials.  For more information, refer to the LinkedIn OAuth Guide.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/linkedin2.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIn the Email or Phone and Password fields, enter your account login credentials respectively and click Sign in.\n\nClick Allow.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nActions\n\nGet an Event Form\n\nSearches\n\nList Event Form Responses\n\nList Event Forms\n\nLinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events\nConnect LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events to Make\nBuild LinkedIn Lead Gen Forms - Events Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

create, update, list, retrieve, and delete the users in your Okta account.\n\nGetting Started with Okta\n\nPrerequisites\n\nAn Okta account\n\nIn order to use Okta with Make, it is necessary to have an Okta account. If you do not have one, you can create an Okta account at okta.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Okta to Make\n\nTo connect your Okta account to Make you need to obtain the API Token from your Okta account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your Okta account.\n\nClick Security > API > Token > Create a Token. Enter a name for the token, and click Create Token.\n\nCopy the Token to your clipboard and click Ok, got it.\n\nGo toMake and open the Okta module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Token field, enter the token copied in step 3.\n\nIn the Host field, enter your organization name. If your Okta account URL address is www.xyz.okta.com then your host is xyz. Click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nUsers\nWatch New Events\nSearch Users\nGet a User\nCreate a User\nUpdate a User\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Users\nOkta\nGetting Started with Okta\nConnecting Okta to Make\nUsers\nWatch New Events\nSearch Users\nGet a User\nCreate a User\nUpdate a User\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Users\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingKlenty\nKlenty\n\nWith Klenty modules in Make, you can manage and monitor the prospects, prospect statuses and cadences in your Klenty account.\n\nTo use the Klenty modules, you must have a paid Klenty account. You can create an account at klenty.com. For subscription information, refer to the Klenty Pricing page.\n\nRefer to the Klenty API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Klenty to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Klenty.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Klenty\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Klenty account:\n\nLog in to your Klenty account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Settings.\n\nIn the Integrations section, click API.\n\nIn the API section, click Generate New.\n\nCopy the appropriate API key:\n\nPersonal API Key to access personal data in your account.\n\nCompany API Key to access data across multiple people in your organization.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Klenty in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Klenty module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nIn the Username field, enter the email address used for creating your Klenty account.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Klenty modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Klenty Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nProspects\n\nWatch Send Prospect\n\nCreate a Prospect\n\nUpdate a Prospect\n\nRemove Prospect Tags\n\nGet a Prospect\n\nSearch Prospects\n\nProspect Status\n\nWatch Prospect Unsubscribe\n\nChange status to DoNotContact\n\nRevert from DoNotContact Status\n\nUnsubscribe a Prospect\n\nGet a Prospect Status\n\nCadence\n\nWatch Replies\n\nWatch Cadence First Reply\n\nWatch Start Cadence\n\nWatch Complete Cadence\n\nWatch Mail Bounce\n\nWatch Opens\n\nWatch Clicks\n\nStart a Cadence\n\nStop a Cadence\n\nStop Mails\n\nResume a Cadence\n\nGet an Email Engagement\n\nGet a StepWise Metric Engagement\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nNote\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nWhen you create a Klenty webhook in Make, it is attached automatically and requires no additional set up.\n\nKlenty\nConnect Klenty to Make\nObtain your API key in Klenty\nEstablish the connection with Klenty in Make\nBuild Klenty Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a JustClick account at justclick.io.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting JustClick to Make\n\nTo connect your JustClick account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your JustClick account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your JustClick account.\n\nClick Your Profile Icon > Profile > Integration.\n\nCopy the API Key to your clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the JustClick module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Username field, enter your account's login username.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied in step 3 and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nTriggers\n\nSee Connecting to JustClick Webhook using Make to add the webhooks in JustClick using Make.\n\nWatch Leads\nWatch Orders\nWatch Purchases\nActions\nAdd a Lead to a List\nRemove a Lead from a List\nUpdate a Lead\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Groups\nConnecting to JustClick Webhook using Make\nJustClick\nGetting Started with JustClick\nConnecting JustClick to Make\nTriggers\nWatch Leads\nWatch Orders\nWatch Purchases\nActions\nAdd a Lead to a List\nRemove a Lead from a List\nUpdate a Lead\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Groups\nConnecting to JustClick Webhook using Make\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can request a demo at iterable.com.\n\nRefer to the Iterable API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nWarning\n\nTo use the Iterable modules, your account must be created on the US domain (app.iterable.com).\n\nConnect Iterable to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Iterable. \n\nEstablish the connection in Make. \n\nObtain your API key in Iterable\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Iterable account:\n\nLog in to your Iterable account.\n\nIn the main dashboard, click Integrations > API Keys.\n\nClick New API key.\n\nEnter a name for the API key and select the permission type.\n\nClick Create API key.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Iterable in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add an Iterable module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Iterable modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Iterable Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nUsers\n\nGet a User\n\nCreate/Update a User\n\nDelete a User\n\nEvents\n\nSearch User Events\n\nTrack an Event\n\nLists\n\nSearch Lists\n\nList Users in a List\n\nCreate a List\n\nAdd a User to a List\n\nDelete a List\n\nRemove a User From List\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nIterable\nConnect Iterable to Make\nObtain your API key in Iterable\nEstablish the connection with Iterable in Make\nBuild Iterable Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Your account must be on the Hypergrowth plan (or above) to access the API key required for connection. You can create an account at app.instantly.ai/auth/signup.\n\nRefer to the Instantly API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Instantly to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Instantly.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Instantly\nNote\n\nYou need to be on the Hypergrowth plan (or above) to be able to access the API key.\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Instantly account:\n\nLog in to your Instantly account.\n\nIn the upper right corner, click your account icon and choose Settings.\n\nClick Integrations > Copy API Key. Store your API key in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Instantly in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add an Instantly module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Instantly modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet Up Instantly Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd an Instantly instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nClick OK.\n\nLog in to your Instantly account.\n\nIn the upper right corner, click your account icon and choose Settings.\n\nClick Integrations > Webhooks > Add Webhook.\n\nIn the Add Webhook field, add the webhook you copied from Make.\n\nChoose your Campaign and Event Type and click Add Webhook.\n\nInstantly will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild Instantly Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nLeads\n\nAdd a Lead to a Campaign\n\nAdd Multiple Leads to a Campaign\n\nSearch Leads\n\nUpdate a Lead Status\n\nRemove a Lead from a Campaign\n\nBlocklist\n\nAdd Entries to the Blocklist\n\nRemove Entries from the Blocklist\n\nOther\n\nWatch Events\n\nMake an API Call\n\nInstantly\nConnect Instantly to Make\nObtain your API key in Instantly\nEstablish the connection with Instantly in Make\nSet Up Instantly Webhooks\nBuild Instantly Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an Instagram account on instagram.com, and then switch the profile to a Business account. For more information, refer to the Meta for Developers Long-Lived Access Token documentation.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/facebook.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Instagram for Business modules. The same applies to Dropbox URLs.\n\nThe username should not start with @, it must match the pattern /^(?!@)/ .\n\nCreate a Reel Post\n\nInstagram Business accounts connected to a Page that requires Page Publishing Authorization (PPA) cannot be published until PPA has been completed.\n\nPhotos or videos must be hosted on a publicly accessible URL and you cannot host your videos on Google Drive even if the file is shared publicly because Instagram API is not able to download files from Google Drive. The same applies to Dropbox URLs.\n\nThe username should not start with @, it must match the pattern /^(?!@)/ .\n\nCreate a Carousel Post\n\nInstagram Business accounts connected to a Page that requires Page Publishing Authorization (PPA) cannot be published until PPA has been completed.\n\nPhotos or videos must be hosted on a publicly accessible URL and you cannot host your videos on Google Drive even if the file is shared publicly because Instagram API is not able to download files from Google Drive. The same applies to Dropbox URLs.\n\nThe username should not start with @, it must match the pattern /^(?!@)/ .\n\nList Media\n\nList Public User Media\n\nGet Media\n\nDownload a Media\n\nGet Album Media\n\nUsers\n\nGet Public User Info\n\nComments\n\nList Media Comments\n\nList Comment Replies\n\nCreate a Comment\n\nCreate a Reply\n\nStories\n\nList Stories\n\nNote\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. You can also reach your admin account at https://example.invisionservice.com/admin if your community URL is https://example.invisionservice.com.\n\nIn the left sidebar under System, go to Site Features > API > REST API Keys.\n\nClick Create New.\n\nEnter a Reference Name for the API key.\n\nIn the Endpoint permissions section, enable the endpoints that will be configured to the API key.\n\nImportant\n\nAfter enabling the required endpoints, configuration to your API key may take some time.\n\nClick Save.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Invision Community in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Invision Community module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nIn the Community field, enter the domain name of your community.\n\nNote\n\nFor communities hosted at Invision: it should be example.invisionservice.com if your URL is https://example.invisionservice.com. If you do not have one, you can create a Growsurf account at growsurf.com/signup.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Growsurf to Make\n\nTo connect your Growsurf account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Growsurf account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLog in to your Growsurf account.\n\nClick Your Profile Icon > Account > Reveal, and copy the API key to your clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the Growsurf module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied in step 2 and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nCampaigns\nWatch Campaign Ended\nList Campaigns\nGet a Campaign\nParticipants\nWatch New Participants\nList Participants\nGet Participants\nCreate a Participant\nUpdate a participant\nDelete a Participant\nParticipant Rewards\nWatch New Participants\nList Participant Rewards\nDelete a Participant Reward\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Participants\nConnecting to Growsurf Webhook using Make\n\nOpen any watch module, enter the details as mentioned in the respective module, click Save and copy the URL address to your clipboard.\n\nLogin to your Growsurf account. Open the campaign whose triggers you want to watch. Click Campaign Actions > Edit Campaign > Options > View All Integrations > Webhooks.\n\nEnter the URL address copied in step 1 and select the options for which you want to recevie the alerts.\n\nThe webhook is successfully enabled.\n\nGrowSurf\nGetting Started with Growsurf\nConnecting Growsurf to Make\nCampaigns\nWatch Campaign Ended\nList Campaigns\nGet a Campaign\nParticipants\nWatch New Participants\nList Participants\nGet Participants\nCreate a Participant\nUpdate a participant\nDelete a Participant\nParticipant Rewards\nWatch New Participants\nList Participant Rewards\nDelete a Participant Reward\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Participants\nConnecting to Growsurf Webhook using Make\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

It is recommended to disable the plugins if you encounter a problem loading a module.\n\nConnect Google Ads Conversions to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Google Ads Conversions module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Customer ID field, enter your customer ID.\n\nYou will find your Customer ID by choosing an account in the Google Ads UI after signing in or clicking on your profile image at the top-right corner of the page. For example: 123-456-7890.\n\nOptional: Switch on the Show advanced settings toggle and enter your Google Cloud Console project client credentials. You can now edit your scenario and add more Google Ads Conversions modules. The Watch activities trigger distinguishes 6 types of posts:\n\nstatus (a text post)\n\narticle (a post with a link to an article)\n\nevent\n\nphoto (a post with a photo)\n\nalbum (a post with an album)\n\nvideo (a post with a link to a video).\n\nConnecting the Google+ service to Make\n\nTo use the above module, you need to connect your Google account to Make. If you do not have a Google account yet, you can create one here.\n\nTo connect your Google account to Make, follow the general instructions for Connecting to services. Make will redirect you to the Google website where you will be prompted to grant Make access to your account:\n\nHere, allow access by clicking the Allow button. Afterwards, you will be redirected back to the Make administration page. Now, you can continue creating your scenario.\n\nPossible problems\nSome information from Google+ is missing\n\nUnfortunately, Google does not provide other applications with the information that is otherwise available via the standard web user interface. For example, you can only import the name and description of an event, and not the start and end date or the location. In the case of an album, you can download only the album name and link, but you cannot download any photo from the album.\n\nThe Watch activities trigger did not download a post (an activity)\n\nMake can only import posts that are public. When publishing a post, the To whom option must be set to Public to make the post accessible also to Make.\n\nGoogle+\nGetting started with Google+\nConnecting the Google+ service to Make\nPossible problems\nSome information from Google+ is missing\nThe Watch activities trigger did not download a post (an activity)\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at goaffpro.com.\n\nRefer to the GoAffPro API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect GoAffPro to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in GoAffPro.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in GoAffPro\n\nTo obtain your API key from your GoAffPro account:\n\nLog in to your GoAffPro account.\n\nClick Add app to store.\n\nSelect Custom SDK as the platform.\n\nEnter your Store Name and Store URL.\n\nClick Submit.\n\nClick Admin Panel.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Settings and go to Advanced.\n\nIn the Access Tokens section, click New API Key.\n\nCopy the X-GOAFFPRO-ACCESS-TOKEN value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with GoAffPro in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a GoAffPro module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more GoAffPro modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild GoAffPro Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nAffiliates\n\nCreate an Affiliate\n\nUpdate an Affiliate\n\nSearch Affiliates\n\nList Affiliates\n\nDelete an Affiliate\n\nRewards\n\nCreate a Reward\n\nUpdate a Reward\n\nList Rewards\n\nDelete a Reward\n\nOrders\n\nCreate an Order\n\nUpdate an Order\n\nList Orders\n\nDelete an Order\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nGoAffPro\nConnect GoAffPro to Make\nObtain your API key in GoAffPro\nEstablish the connection with GoAffPro in Make\nBuild GoAffPro Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at  ads.google.com\n\nRefer to the Google Ads API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nNote\n\nMake's use and transfer of information received from Google APIs to any other app will adhere to Google API Services User Data Policy.\n\nImportant\n\nSome adblocking browser plugins could block the Google Ads Lead Forms module. It is recommended to disable the plugins if you encounter a problem loading a module.\n\nConnect Google Ads Lead Forms to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Google Ads Lead Forms module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection. To create a webhook, you will need your Customer ID and your Lead Form ID.\n\nYou can find your Customer ID by choosing an account in the Google Ads UI after signing in or clicking on your profile image at the top-right corner of the page. For example: 123-456-7890.\n\nYou can find your Lead Form ID by logging in to Google Ads, navigating to Ads & Extensions > Extensions > Lead Form Extensions and choosing the extension you wish to find the ID for.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Customer ID field, enter your customer ID.\n\nOptional: Switch on the Show advanced settings toggle and enter your Google Cloud Console project client credentials. For more information, see the Create and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Ads Lead Forms section below.\n\nClick Sign in with Google.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Google Ads Lead Forms modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Ads Lead Forms\nBuild Google Ads Lead Forms Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nTriggers\n\nWatch Lead Forms\n\nNote\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nWhen you create a Google Ads Lead Forms webhook in Make, it is attached automatically and requires no additional set up.\n\nGoogle Ads Lead Forms\nConnect Google Ads Lead Forms to Make\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Ads Lead Forms\nBuild Google Ads Lead Forms Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a Gist account at app.getgist.com/signup.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Gist to Make\n\nTo connect your Gist account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Gist account.\n\nLog in to your Gist account.\n\nGo to Settings > API key.\n\nClick on the Copy button to copy the API Key to your clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the Gist module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nEnter the API Key to the respective field and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nWatch Events\n\nTriggers when specified events are performed.\n\nNote\n\nThe module functionality is available only for users who have subscribed to the Gist PRO plan.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook. E.g. Meeting Scheduled.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Gist account.\n\nAssigning the Gist event to the Make Watch Events module\n\nGo to Make and open the Gist Watch Events module's settings.\n\nCreate a Webhook and copy the provided webhook URL.\n\nLog in to your Gist account.\n\nGo to Settings > Webhooks.\n\nClick on the New Webhook button.\n\nEnter a name for the webhook. E.g. User Created.\n\nSwitch on the Active button.\n\nEnter the webhook URL you have copied in step 2 above to the Endpoint URL field.\n\nSelect the event(s) that will trigger the Gist Watch Events module in Make and click the Save button.\n\nNow, when a user is created, the Watch Events module in Make is triggered.\n\nUsers\nCreate User\nUpdate User\nFetch User\nList Users\nDelete User\nLeads\nCreate Lead\nUpdate Lead\nFetch Lead\nList Leads\nDelete Lead\nTags\nCreate Tag\nUpdate Tag\nTag/Untag Users or Leads\nList Tags\nDelete Tag\nSegments\nFetch Segment\nList Segments\nCampaigns\nFetch Campaign\nList Campaigns\nTracked Events\nRecord Tracked Event\nList Tracked Events\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Users\nGist\nGetting Started with Gist\nConnecting Gist to Make\nWatch Events\nAssigning the Gist event to the Make Watch Events module\nUsers\nCreate User\nUpdate User\nFetch User\nList Users\nDelete User\nLeads\nCreate Lead\nUpdate Lead\nFetch Lead\nList Leads\nDelete Lead\nTags\nCreate Tag\nUpdate Tag\nTag/Untag Users or Leads\nList Tags\nDelete Tag\nSegments\nFetch Segment\nList Segments\nCampaigns\nFetch Campaign\nList Campaigns\nTracked Events\nRecord Tracked Event\nList Tracked Events\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Users\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingFreshmarketer\nFreshmarketer\n\nWith Freshmarketer modules in Make, you can create, update, retrieve, subscribe, unsubscribe, delete, or search contacts and lists in your Freshmarketer account.\n\nTo use the Freshmarketer modules, you must have a Freshmarketer account. You can create a Freshmarketer account at https://www.freshmarketer.com/signup.\n\nRefer to the Freshmarketer API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Freshmarketer to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Freshmarketer.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Freshmarketer\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Freshmarketer account:\n\nLog in to your Freshmarketer account.\n\nClick the Settings icon in the left navigation. Then choose Admin Settings.\n\nOn the Admin Settings page, under Website Tracking and APIs, click API Settings.\n\nConfirm that you wish to view your API.\n\nCopy the API Key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Freshmarketer in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Freshmarketer module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Domain Name field, enter your domain name. For example, if your Freshmarketer URL is https://xyz-org.freshmarketer.com/mas/#/ then your domain name is xyz-org.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Freshmarketer modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Freshmarketer Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nContacts\n\nWatch Contacts\n\nUpsert a Contact\n\nView a Contact\n\nList Contacts\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nDelete a Contact\n\nLists\n\nAdd a List\n\nList Lists\n\nList Contacts in List\n\nSubscribe a Contact to a List\n\nUnsubscribe Contacts from a List\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nFreshmarketer\nConnect Freshmarketer to Make\nObtain your API key in Freshmarketer\nEstablish the connection with Freshmarketer in Make\nBuild Freshmarketer Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Loyalty\nYotpo - Referrals\nYouTube\nZendesk Sell\nZeroBounce\nZoho Campaigns\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsMarketingFacebook Conversions API for CRM\nFacebook Conversions API for CRM\n\nWith the Facebook Conversion API for CRM modules in Make, you can create lead events.\n\nTo get started with the Facebook Conversions API for CRM app:\n\ncreate a Facebook account\n\ncreate a Facebook Business Manager account at business.facebook.com\n\ncreate a new pixel specifically for the lead events in your Facebook Event Manager. The pixel should be of type CRM.\n\nstart sending simple \"Lead\" events with the Facebook Conversions API app immediately after you receive leads with Facebook Leads Ads app. More info can be found in the video below.\n\nstart sending lead status change events via Make to Facebook with the Facebook Conversions API for CRM app. The Facebook account used during the connection creation should be the admin of the Facebook Ads account and the newly created pixel.\n\nafter a week or so, you need to go to the Pixel's Settings and finish the configuration of your sales funnel to define the lead status that will be used for optimizing your Facebook Lead Ads Campaigns where the optimization is set to Facebook Conversions API for CRM.\n\nMake strongly recommends watching the video below to understand the above prerequisites before you start using the app.\n\nNote\n\nAs mentioned in the video, in order to be able to use the Facebook Conversions API for CRM app, you first need to start capturing Facebook lead IDs in your CRM. To do so, you can start using the Facebook Lead Ads app on Make.\n\nThis app allows you to listen for new form submissions on Facebook and then pass the form data along with the Lead ID to your CRM. For more information, see the Facebook Lead Ads app.\n\nConnect Facebook Conversions API for CRM to Make\n\nTo connect to the Facebook Conversions API for CRM app:\n\nLog in to your Make account, insert a Facebook Conversions API for CRM module in your scenario, and click the Add button next to the Connection field.\n\nOptional: Click Show Advanced Settings to enter the client credentials of your custom application.\n\nAdd the details as provided below to connect the app:\n\nConnection name\n\n\t\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the connection.\n\n\n\n\nYour Business Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter your business name.\n\n\n\n\nCurrency\n\n\t\n\nSelect the applicable currency for your business. For example, USD.\n\n\n\n\nTimezone\n\n\t\n\nSelect the timezone applicable to your business.\n\n\n\n\nExternal Business ID\n\n\t\n\nOptional: Enter a unique Business ID.\n\nNote\n\nMake strongly recommends entering an External Business ID as a unique identifier to distinguish multiple businesses.\n\nThis field is mandatory if you want to create multiple connections to multiple Facebook Business accounts.\n\nThe ID can be any string of your choice but ensure the ID is unique for your different businesses if you run more than one business.\n\nFor example, fubar-123 is for a business called Fubar.\n\n\n\n\nClient ID and Client Secret\n\n\t\n\nOptional: Client credentials of your custom application.\n\nClick Save and select your account settings for the connection.\n\nNote\n\nThe connection setup could take up to 3 - 5 minutes.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenarioand add more Facebook Conversions API for CRM modules. If your connection needs reauthorization, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nList of modules to start with in scenarios with the most common CRM apps\n\nStart by selecting one of the following CRM modules you want to connect to Facebook and upload lead events.\n\nThe following table provides the apps and the modules to start with these apps using Make:\n\nCRM\n\n\t\n\nModule to Start With\n\n\t\n\nNotes\n\n\n\n\nHubSpot\n\n\t\n\nWatch Records\n\n\t\n\nMonitors both creations and updates\n\n\n\n\nSalesforce\n\n\t\n\nWatch Records\n\n\t\n\nMonitors both creations and updates\n\n\n\n\nZoho\n\n\t\n\nWatch Objects\n\n\t\n\nMonitors both creations and updates\n\n\n\n\nBitrix\n\n\t\n\nWatch Leads/Deals\n\n\t\n\nThe modules should be set to watch by modified time.\n\n\n\n\nMicrosoft Dynamics\n\n\t\n\nSearch Records\n\n\t\n\nThe Watch Records will only give you creations but not updates, so you will have to go with search and filter for records that have been edited since the last run.\n\nActions\n\nYou can create events with the following module.\n\nCreate a Lead Event\n\nCreates a specific lead.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Facebook Conversions API for CRM account.\n\n\n\n\nEvent Name\n\n\t\n\nName of the event to capture the stages you use within your CRM.\n\nEnsure to send all stages as they are updated, including the initial lead stage.\n\nFor example, your stages may include the following types.\n\nIf a lead reaches the final, Converted stage, all previous stages should have been sent beforehand.\n\nInitial Lead from FB\n\nMarketing Qualified Lead\n\nSales Opportunity\n\nConverted\n\nFacebook recommends using a variable to pass in the stages from your database. Alternatively, you could create a separate API call for each stage.\n\n\n\n\nEvent Time\n\n\t\n\nA timestamp that indicates when your CRM updates the lead stage update event.\n\nFacebook recommends using a variable to pass in the Unix timestamp values from your database.\n\nNote\n\nThe event_time parameter value can be up to 7 days before you send an event to Facebook.\n\n\n\n\nLead ID\n\n\t\n\nThe FB generated ID for every lead, a 15 or 16-digit number.\n\nIt is required to use Lead IDs instead of customer information for matching. Facebook recommends using a variable to pass in the ID values from your database.\n\nLead ID associated with a lead generated by Facebook's Lead Ads. This means you can only use this module when your lead originally came from Lead Ads, and you saved its Lead ID.\n\n\n\n\nLead Event Source\n\n\t\n\nName of the tool where the leads are coming from.\n\nWe suggest you use Make or anything regarding your business process. You can also use the name of the true source system. For example, CRMs such as Hubspot, Salesforce, Pipedrive, etc.,\n\n\n\n\nPixel ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect or map the Pixel ID of your Facebook account. To create and set up the Pixel ID, refer to Facebook help page.\n\nLeave this field empty for the pixel ID you picked when creating or reauthorizing the connection. If you want a pixel under a different Facebook Business Manager account, create a new connection instead.\n\nFor more information, see the Facebook Conversions API for CRM Integration page.\n\nFacebook Conversions API for CRM\nConnect Facebook Conversions API for CRM to Make\nList of modules to start with in scenarios with the most common CRM apps\nActions\nCreate a Lead Event\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can an account at account.google.com.\n\nRefer to the Firebase Cloud Messaging API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Google Chrome to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Google Chrome module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Switch on the Show advanced settings toggle and enter your Google Cloud Console project client credentials. For more information, see the Create and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Chrome section below.\n\nClick Sign in with Google.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Chrome\nBuild Firebase Cloud Messaging Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nActions\n\nSend a Message\n\nFirebase Cloud Messaging\nConnect Google Chrome to Make\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Chrome\nBuild Firebase Cloud Messaging Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."
